1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Map Test Coverage Gaps in Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/kafka--e678b4b (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/kafka--e678b4b (mirror of apache/kafka)
**Output:** Write your analysis to `/workspace/coverage_analysis.md`

## Objective

Identify test coverage gaps in Kafka's consumer group coordinator. The group coordinator manages consumer group membership, partition assignment, and offset commits for Kafka consumers.

## Scope

Focus on:
- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.scala` — main coordinator logic
- `core/src/test/scala/unit/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorTest.scala` — existing tests
- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadata.scala` — group state machine

## Content Expectations

Your analysis must:
1. **Identify at least 5 specific failure modes** that are not tested in `GroupCoordinatorTest.scala`
2. **Propose a regression test** for each failure mode (class name, test method signature, key assertions)
3. **Estimate the coverage delta** each proposed test would add (which code paths would it hit)
4. **Label risk level**: HIGH / MEDIUM / LOW

## Output Format

Write to `/workspace/coverage_analysis.md`:

```markdown
# Test Coverage Gap Analysis: Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

## Summary

## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests

### Failure Mode 1: [Name]
- **Risk**: HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW
- **Code Location**: GroupCoordinator.scala ~line NNN
- **Description**: [What failure scenario is untested]
- **Proposed Test**:
  ```java
  @Test
  public void testXxx() { ... }
  ```
- **Coverage Delta**: [Which code paths this test would exercise]

[Repeat for 5+ failure modes]

## File References
```

- Each gap must reference a specific file and approximate location
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

     4→
     5→Analysis of `GroupMetadataManager.java` (~7500 lines), `OffsetMetadataManager.java` (~1000 lines), and `GroupCoordinatorShard.java` (~1500 lines) reveals 67 existing unit tests in `GroupMetadataManagerTest.java`. However, several critical failure modes and edge cases around authorization, concurrent state transitions, and error handling paths remain under-tested. The coordinator manages three group types (Consumer, Classic, Share, Streams) with complex state machines, and the integration points between group metadata and offset operations introduce race conditions that are not adequately covered.

     8→
     9→## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests
    10→
    11→### Failure Mode 1: Offset Commit Authorization Denial with Stale Member Removal
    12→
    13→**Risk**: MEDIUM
    14→
    15→**Code Location**:
    16→- OffsetMetadataManager.java ~line 614 (`validateOffsetCommit` method)
    17→- GroupMetadataManager.java ~line 1500-1600 (member removal/fencing logic)
    18→
    19→**Description**:
    20→When a consumer group member's epoch becomes stale and the member is removed from the group's current assignment, a concurrent offset commit request from that member should be rejected with `ILLEGAL_GENERATION` error. However, there is no test that validates the interaction between:
    21→1. Member being fenced/removed from group state
    22→2. Concurrent offset commit attempt from that fenced member
    23→3. Authorization context validation failure
    24→
    25→This gap exists because existing tests either test successful offset commits or test member removal in isolation, but not the ordering and race conditions.

## Implementation Recommendations

.setGenerationIdOrMemberEpoch(1)\n                    .setTopics(List.of(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n                        .setName(\"topic-1\")\n                        .setPartitions(List.of(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                            .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                            .setCommittedOffset(200)\n                            .setCommittedMetadata(\"\"))))));\n\n        // Verify commit either succeeds cleanly or fails with GROUP_ID_NOT_FOUND\n        // but doesn't create inconsistent state\n        OffsetCommitResponseData response = result.response();\n        for (OffsetCommitResponseData.OffsetCommitResponseTopic topic : response.topics()) {\n            for commitThread.start();\n    deleteThread.start();\n\n    commitThread.join(5000);\n    deleteThread.join(5000);\n\n    assertFalse(commitThread.isAlive(), \"Commit thread deadlocked\");\n    assertFalse(deleteThread.isAlive(), \"Delete thread deadlocked\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests concurrent group deletion and offset commit operations\n- Validates synchronization in affected groups. Heartbeat that changes subscription\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topic1Id, 0, 1))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> heartbeatResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId)\n            .setMemberEpoch(1)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topic1Name)));\n\n    int epochAfterHeartbeat = context.groupEpoch(groupId);\n\n    // 2. Offset metadata being persisted when it shouldn't be\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testOffsetCommitWithMixedValidAndInvalidMetadata() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext context = new OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder().build();\n\n    String oversizedMetadata = \"x\".repeat(OffsetMetadataManager.OFFSET_METADATA_MAX_SIZE + 1);\n\n    OffsetCommitRequestData request = new OffsetCommitRequestData()\n        .setGroupId(groupId)\n        .setMemberId(\"member-1\")\n        .setGenerationIdOrMemberEpoch(1)\n        .setTopics(List.of(\n            new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n                .setName(\"topic-1\")\n                .setPartitions(List.of(\n                    new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                        .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                        .setCommittedOffset(100)\n                        .setCommittedMetadata(\"valid-metadata\"),\n                    new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                        .setPartitionIndex(1)\n                        .setCommittedOffset(200)\n                        .setCommittedMetadata(oversizedMetadata))),\n            new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n                .setName(\"topic-2\")\n                .setPartitions(List.of(\n                    new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                        .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                        .setCommittedOffset(300)\n                        .setCommittedMetadata(\"another-valid\")))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<OffsetCommitResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result =\n        context.offsetMetadataManager.commitOffset(requestContext(), request);\n\n    // Verify mixed response\n    OffsetCommitResponseData response = result.response();\n    assertEquals(2, response.topics().size());\n\n    // topic-1 should have one success and one error\n    OffsetCommitResponseData.OffsetCommitResponseTopic topic1 = response.topics().get(0);\n    assertEquals(2, topic1.partitions().size());\n    assertEquals(Errors.NONE.code(), topic1.partitions().get(0).errorCode());\n    assertEquals(Errors.OFFSET_METADATA_TOO_LARGE.code(), topic1.partitions().get(1).errorCode());\n\n    // topic-2 should succeed\n    OffsetCommitResponseData.OffsetCommitResponseTopic topic2 = response.topics().get(1);\n    assertEquals(1, topic2.partitions().size());\n    assertEquals(Errors.NONE.code(), topic2.partitions().get(0).errorCode());\n\n    // Verify only valid commits are in records\n    assertEquals(2, result.records().size()); // 2 valid partitions\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests the loop at line 621-663 with mixed valid/invalid partitions\n- Validates response construction for partial failure scenarios\n- Ensures invalid metadata is rejected without affecting valid commits\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Consumer Group Heartbeat with Invalid Regular Expression During State 0)\n\nHowever, it does NOT test:\n- Invalid regex when member state is UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS or UNASSIGNED (mid-rebalance)\n- Invalid regex when group is in PREPARING_REBALANCE state\n- Invalid regex context.offsetMetadataManager.commitTransactionalOffset(requestContext(), request);\n\n    // Should convert to ILLEGAL_GENERATION error, not propagate StaleMemberEpochException\n 5: Group Deletion Race with Active Offset Commit\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**:\n- GroupMetadataManager.java ~line 8200+ (deleteGroup method)\n- OffsetMetadataManager.java ~line 610 (commitOffset validation)\n\n**Description**:\nThe `deleteGroup` operation removes group from the groups map and marks it as DEAD. Thread B: Processes offset commit (checks group exists in groups map at line 614's `validateOffsetCommit`)\n3. Thread B: Commit succeeds and records are generated\n4. Group state is inconsistent - marked DEAD but with new offset records\n\nThe existing tests don't cover the timing where `deleteGroup` happens concurrently with `commitOffset`, especially when:\n- Delete returns before offset commit's validation completes\n- Offset records are appended after group is deleted\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testOffsetCommitRaceWithGroupDeletion() throws Exception {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId = \"member-1\";\n\n    OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext context = new OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder().build();\n\n    // Create group and commit offset\n    context.offsetMetadataManager.commitOffset(\n        requestContext(),\n        new OffsetCommitRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId)\n            .setGenerationIdOrMemberEpoch(1)\n            .setTopics(List.of(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n                .setName(\"topic-1\")\n                .setPartitions(List.of(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                    .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                    .setCommittedOffset(100)\n                    .setCommittedMetadata(\"\"))))));\n\n    // Simulate concurrent delete\n    CountDownLatch deleteStarted = new CountDownLatch(1);\n    CountDownLatch commitCanContinue = new CountDownLatch(1);\n\n    Thread deleteThread = new Thread(() -> {\n        deleteStarted.countDown();\n        try {\n            commitCanContinue.await();\n        } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n        }\n        // Delete group\n        context.groupMetadataManager.deleteGroup(groupId);\n    });\n\n    // Attempt another commit while delete is in progress\n    Thread commitThread = new Thread(() -> {\n        try {\n            deleteStarted.await();\n            // Give delete time to start but not complete\n            Thread.sleep(10);\n        } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n        }\n\n        CoordinatorResult<OffsetCommitResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result =\n            context.offsetMetadataManager.commitOffset(\n                requestContext(),\n                new OffsetCommitRequestData()\n                    .setGroupId(groupId)\n                    .setMemberId(memberId)\n                    .setGenerationIdOrMemberEpoch(1)\n                    .setTopics(List.of(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n                        .setName(\"topic-1\")\n                        .setPartitions(List.of(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                            .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                            .setCommittedOffset(200)\n                            .setCommittedMetadata(\"\"))))));\n\n        // Verify commit either succeeds cleanly or fails with GROUP_ID_NOT_FOUND\n        // but doesn't create inconsistent state\n        OffsetCommitResponseData response = result.response();\n        for (OffsetCommitResponseData.OffsetCommitResponseTopic topic : response.topics()) {\n            for (OffsetCommitResponseData.OffsetCommitResponsePartition partition : topic.partitions()) {\n                Errors error = Errors.forCode(partition.errorCode());\n                assertTrue(error == Errors.NONE || error == Errors.GROUP_ID_NOT_FOUND,\n                    \"Unexpected error code: \" + error);\n            }\n        }\n\n        commitCanContinue.countDown();\n    });\n\n    commitThread.start();\n    deleteThread.start();\n\n    commitThread.join(5000);\n    deleteThread.join(5000);\n\n    assertFalse(commitThread.isAlive(), \"Commit thread deadlocked\");\n    assertFalse(deleteThread.isAlive(), \"Delete thread deadlocked\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests concurrent group deletion and offset commit operations\n- Validates synchronization in GroupMetadataManager.deleteGroup() and OffsetMetadataManager.commitOffset()\n- Ensures no state machine corruption under race conditions\n- Exercises error paths for GROUP_ID_NOT_FOUND\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 6: Consumer Group Epoch Bump During Metadata Update Race\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**:\n- GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 3200-3300 (consumer group rebalance trigger)\n- Heartbeat that changes subscription\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topic1Id, 0, 1))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> heartbeatResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId)\n            .setMemberEpoch(1)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topic1Name)));\n\n    int epochAfterHeartbeat = context.groupEpoch(groupId);\n\n    // 2. # Test Coverage Gap Analysis: Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

## Summary

Analysis of `GroupMetadataManager.java` (~7500 lines), `OffsetMetadataManager.java` (~1000 lines), and `GroupCoordinatorShard.java` (~1500 lines) reveals 67 existing unit tests in `GroupMetadataManagerTest.java`. However, several critical failure modes and edge cases around authorization, concurrent state transitions, and error handling paths remain under-tested. The coordinator manages three group types (Consumer, Classic, Share, Streams) with complex state machines, and the integration points between group metadata and offset operations introduce race conditions that are not adequately covered.

---

## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests

### Failure Mode 1: Offset Commit Authorization Denial with Stale Member Removal

**Risk**: MEDIUM

**Code Location**:
- OffsetMetadataManager.java ~line 614 (`validateOffsetCommit` method)
- GroupMetadataManager.java ~line 1500-1600 (member removal/fencing logic)

**Description**:
When a consumer group member's epoch becomes stale and the member is removed from the group's current assignment, a concurrent offset commit request from that member should be rejected with `ILLEGAL_GENERATION` error. However, there is no test that validates the interaction between:
1. Member being fenced/removed from group state
2. Concurrent offset commit attempt from that fenced member
3. Authorization context validation failure

This gap exists because existing tests either test successful offset commits or test member removal in isolation, but not the ordering and race conditions.

**Proposed Test**:
```java
@Test
public void testOffsetCommitAfterMemberIsRemoved() {
    String groupId = "test-group";
    String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();
    String topic = "test-to
... (truncated)
